without this, `cdk synth` would fall back to the SDK default credential chain even when the rest of the migration ran under the named profile. **Shared `STABLE_TERMINAL_STATUSES`**: extracted into [src/cli/cfn-stack-states.ts](src/cli/cfn-stack-states.ts) (`ReadonlySet<string>` of `CREATE_COMPLETE` / `UPDATE_COMPLETE` / `UPDATE_ROLLBACK_COMPLETE` / `IMPORT_COMPLETE` / `IMPORT_ROLLBACK_COMPLETE`) so `cdkd migrate`'s pre-flight check and `cdkd import --migrate-from-cloudformation`'s retirement flow consume one source-of-truth instead of the pre-PR "kept in sync" honor-system docstring. **Spec validation findings** documented in [docs/design/465-cfn-migrate.md](docs/design/465-cfn-migrate.md) "Empirical validation (2026-05-22)" section based on a manual `cdk migrate --from-path` run against a 3-resource fixture template: (a) source logical IDs are PRESERVED exactly in the synth template (no hash suffix in the typical case), (b) `Metadata.aws:cdk:path` shape: `<StackName>/<LogicalId>` — last `/`-separated segment is the source logical ID, (c) Properties values match source (top-level key order differs — synth alphabetizes; Tags array order preserved), (d) `migrate.json` (generated by `cdk migrate`) is NOT a mapping file — only `{"//":"...","Source":"localfile"|"<other>"}`, (e) CDK synth adds 4 things PR B's mapping layer must skip: `AWS::CDK::Metadata` resource (already excluded by `src/cli/cdk-path.ts`), `Conditions.CDKMetadataAvailable`, `Parameters.BootstrapVersion`, `Rules.CheckBootstrapVersion`. **New error classes** in [src/utils/error-handler.ts](src/utils/error-handler.ts): `MissingCdkCliError` (exit 1) + `LocalMigrateError` (exit 2). Tests: 76+ new across 6 unit test files at [tests/unit/cli/commands/migrate/](tests/unit/cli/commands/migrate/) covering version-parse / pre-flight reject matrix / output-dir guard / spawn argv assembly + signal-termination / synth + parse paths / orchestrator full happy path + profile threading + GetTemplate-failure hard-error + cliCheck.warn + SAM/Include INFO branches + skipInstall-default + cdk-missing-first-check + CR-reject / output-dir-clash / skipSynth-returns-null. Smoke integ at [tests/integration/migrate-from-bare-cfn-codegen-only/](tests/integration/migrate-from-bare-cfn-codegen-only/) (AWS-free, ~30s local): pinned `aws-cdk@2.1112.0` devDep + `pnpm install --ignore-workspace` to keep the cdkd-repo's pnpm-workspace from hoisting the version, then `pnpm exec cdk migrate --from-path ./template-fixture.json` and asserts the generated `cdk.json` / `lib/<x>-stack.ts` exist, `cdk synth` succeeds, the 3 source logical IDs (`S3Bucket` / `SsmParam` / `SnsTopic`) appear in the synth template each with `Metadata.aws:cdk:path: SmokeMigrated/<logicalId>`, AND the source Properties round-trip cleanly through CDK's L1 codegen.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-api` honors authorizers on HTTP API v2 service-integration routes (closes [#502](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/502); also fixes [#512](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/512) stale `/v1/unsupported` assertion in the same integ fixture). Pre-PR the dispatcher in [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) ran the SDK call BEFORE the authorizer pass would fire, AND [src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts](src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts) `attachAuthorizers` skipped `serviceIntegration` routes entirely — so a CDK app that wired a JWT / Lambda / Cognito / IAM authorizer to e.g. `POST /sqs` silently let every local request reach the AWS SDK call without authentication, asymmetric with AWS-deployed behavior. Post-PR three structural changes close the gap: (1) **`attachAuthorizers`** drops the `route.serviceIntegration` skip — every route gets its authorizer attached regardless of whether the dispatch target is a Lambda or an SDK adapter. (2) **`handleRequest`** in [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) reorders the per-request pipeline so the authorizer pass runs **BEFORE** the service-integration short-circuit (the snapshot / matchCtx / baseEvent construction is hoisted above the dispatch branch); a deny aborts the request with 401 / 403 and never reaches the SDK adapter, symmetric with how Lambda routes already worked. (3) **`RequestParameterContext`** in [src/local/parameter-mapping.ts](src/local/parameter-mapping.ts) gains a new optional `authorizer?: Readonly<Record<string, unknown>>` field, and `resolveSingleReference` recognizes `$context.authorizer.<path>` selection expressions — so an SDK adapter's `RequestParameters` can carry e.g. `MessageAttributes: '${context.authorizer.jwt.claims.sub}'` and the authorizer's claims / context / principalId round-trip into the SDK call. Per-authorizer-kind shape mirrors `applyAuthorizerOverlay`'s event-level overlay: Lambda authorizers (TOKEN / REQUEST / IAM) flatten `principalId` + context fields at the top level (`$context.authorizer.principalId` / `$context.authorizer.<key>`); Cognito (REST v1) nests claims under `$context.authorizer.claims.<key>`; JWT (HTTP v2) nests claims under `$context.authorizer.jwt.claims.<key>` with `$context.authorizer.jwt.scopes` (always present, may be empty). The new helper `buildAuthorizerContextForServiceIntegration` in [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) (exported for unit testing) is the single source of truth for that shape. Nested-path traversal uses dot-separated walk (shared with `resolveBodyJsonPath`'s pattern); non-string leaves stringify with `JSON.stringify` so they round-trip into SDK string-typed inputs. The pre-PR `warnIgnoredServiceIntegrationAuthorizers` boot warn and the `findIgnoredServiceIntegrationAuthorizers` helper are removed entirely — the gap they were warning about is closed structurally. **Bundled fix for [#512](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/512)**: the existing `tests/integration/local-start-api/lib/local-start-api-stack.ts` fixture's `/v1/unsupported` route was switched from HTTP_PROXY (first-class since PR #505) to a direct-AWS-service integration (`Integration.Type: 'AWS'` with an `arn:aws:apigateway:<region>:s3:path/...` Uri) — cdkd's REST v1 classifier correctly surfaces this as deferred-501 with the "non-Lambda service ... not emulated locally" reason, restoring the 501 assertion's signal value. **Implementation**: [src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts](src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts) (drop the skip + remove the helper / interface), [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) (reorder + new helper + extended `handleServiceIntegrationRequest` signature), [src/local/parameter-mapping.ts](src/local/parameter-mapping.ts) (new `authorizer` field + `$context.authorizer.X` resolution + `resolveAuthorizerPath` helper), [src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts) (remove `warnIgnoredServiceIntegrationAuthorizers` call and import). Tests: 4 new in [tests/unit/local/authorizer-resolver.test.ts](tests/unit/local/authorizer-resolver.test.ts) (JWT + Lambda REQUEST + NONE + missing-AuthorizationType all on service-integration routes); 7 new in [tests/unit/local/parameter-mapping.test.ts](tests/unit/local/parameter-mapping.test.ts) (`$context.authorizer.X` matrix: Lambda principalId / JWT claims / Cognito claims / missing path / no authorizer / non-string-leaf stringify / `${...}` interpolation); 9 new in [tests/unit/local/http-server.test.ts](tests/unit/local/http-server.test.ts) (`buildAuthorizerContextForServiceIntegration` matrix: undefined inputs / Lambda TOKEN+REQUEST / IAM / Cognito / JWT / no principalId / empty context). Integ fixture at [tests/integration/local-start-api/](tests/integration/local-start-api/) extended with a Lambda-authorizer-protected `POST /protected-sqs` route (reuses the existing `/protected` route's authorizer Lambda — Allow on `Authorization: Bearer let-me-in`); `verify.sh` asserts (a) missing Bearer → 401 (the SDK never fires), (b) valid Bearer → SDK dispatches (non-401, non-501 — typically 4xx from the missing fixture queue), and the route's `RequestParameters` carries a `$context.authorizer.principalId` reference proving the authorizer context is plumbed into the parameter-mapping context.

- ✅ Follow-up minors from PR (#505) review on REST v1 non-AWS_PROXY integrations (closes (#507)). Eight maintenance items deferred during the (#505) blocker fix-back, all targeted at `src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts` + `src/local/integration-response-selector.ts` + `src/local/vtl-engine.ts`. (1) **ContainerPool release in `finally`** ([src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts](src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts) `dispatchAwsLambdaIntegration`) — wraps every post-`pool.acquire(...)` path (including the VTL response-template evaluation that lives outside the existing `invokeRie` try / catch) in `try { ... } finally { pool.release(handle); }`, so a throw on the synchronous `selectIntegrationResponse` / `pickResponseTemplate` / `evaluateVtl` block no longer strands the warm container. Matches the buffered AWS_PROXY path's pattern in [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts). (2) **Dead `urlObj` parameter dropped** on `applyRequestParameters` — the querystring / path-rewrite branches were always warn-and-skip, the parameter never resolved against a URL, and every call site passed `urlObj: undefined`; dropping the field removes the misleading shape without changing behavior. (3) **Debug log on `extractStatusCodeFromRendered` fallback** — pre-fix the helper silently returned `undefined` when the rendered MOCK request template was not JSON or did not carry `{statusCode: N}`, so users diagnosing a MOCK dispatch had no signal why their selection driver was unparseable. Post-fix `logger.debug` names the offending rendered output (truncated to 200 chars) with the per-branch reason. (4) **MOCK Content-Type omitted on empty body** — `dispatchMockIntegration` now strips `Content-Type` from the response headers when `body === ''` AND the value is still the default-initializer `application/json`. ResponseParameters overlays that set Content-Type to an explicit literal are preserved (load-bearing for the rare empty-body-with-explicit-text case). (5) **Header vs querystring case-sensitivity documentation** — `applyRequestParameters` / `resolveRequestParameterValue` in [src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts](src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts) and `buildVtlInput` `$input.params` in [src/local/vtl-engine.ts](src/local/vtl-engine.ts) each gain a docstring section spelling out the AWS-deployed semantics (headers case-insensitive + multi-value comma-joined; querystring case-sensitive + last-wins; path case-sensitive) with cross-links between the read / write halves. (6) **`Number.isInteger` over `parseInt`** with HTTP `[100, 600)` range guard — both `extractStatusCodeFromRendered` (in `rest-v1-integrations.ts`) and `parseStatus` (the helper in `integration-response-selector.ts` AND its local twin in `rest-v1-integrations.ts`) switch from `Number.parseInt(val, 10)` to `Number(val) + Number.isInteger(parsed) + 100 ≤ n < 600`, so a malformed `statusCode: "200abc"` / fractional `200.5` / empty `""` / whitespace `"   "` / negative `"-1"` / out-of-range `"999"` / `"0x10"` (= 16) all reject to `undefined` (or the caller's fallback) and the dispatcher falls back to the default `IntegrationResponses[]` entry instead of silently emitting HTTP 0 / 16 / negative status codes. (7) **VTL `$input.json` against a non-JSON body** — pre-fix `lazyJson()` swallowed the parse failure and returned `null`, so a non-JSON body silently produced `null` slices that downstream `#if($input.json('$.x'))` interpreted as the empty case. Post-fix `lazyJson({ throwOnParseError: true })` (consulted ONLY by `$input.json(...)`; `$input.path(...)` keeps the lenient null fallback) throws a `VtlEvaluationError` with a clear message; the existing `vtlFailure` catch in every dispatcher routes the throw to a 502 with the template + reason in the body — matches AWS's 400 + `{"message":"Invalid JSON request body"}` outcome with cdkd's standard VTL-failure shape. (8) **`looseEqual` docstring** in [src/local/vtl-engine.ts](src/local/vtl-engine.ts) — documents the cross-type compare semantics (Velocity-style coerce-via-`String()` rather than JavaScript's `==` operator) and links to the official Velocity spec at <https://velocity.apache.org/engine/2.0/vtl-reference.html#a3.4.4.RelationalOperators>. **Single-source ResponseParameters header overlay**: `evaluateResponseParameters` normalizes every overlay header key to lowercase at the emit layer so dispatcher-default seeds (always lowercase) and user overlays converge cleanly — pre-fix the empty-body Content-Type drop in `dispatchMockIntegration` could leak a PascalCase `Content-Type` to the wire when the user's ResponseParameters used mixed case. Tests: 29 unit cases across [tests/unit/local/rest-v1-integrations-issue-507.test.ts](tests/unit/local/rest-v1-integrations-issue-507.test.ts) covering release-in-finally + VTL throw + invoke error + acquire failure (item 1); debug log emission + offending-output truncation (item 3); Content-Type drop / preserve / explicit-literal-overlay + case-distinct keys collapse (item 4); the full `parseStatus` / `extractStatusCodeFromRendered` boundary matrix `""` / `"   "` / `"-1"` / `"99"` / `"999"` / `"100"` / `"599"` (item 6); `$input.json` throws on non-JSON body / `$input.path` lenient fallback / `$input.json` happy path / empty body (item 7). Items 2 / 5 / 8 are docstring / dead-code-removal only (no test additions).

- ✅ Fix: `cdkd local start-api` RESPONSE_STREAM hardening (closes [#503](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/503), follow-up minors from PR #501 review). Three small but load-bearing edges in the streaming Function URL path: (1) **`invokeRieStreaming` JSDoc clarifies total-wall-time timeout semantics** — the single armed `setTimeout(timeoutMs, controller.abort)` bounds prelude wait AND body drain together, so a legitimately long-lived stream (e.g. 15-min AI / LLM proxy) will be torn down mid-body when the timer fires even though bytes are arriving correctly. Callers must size `timeoutMs` to cover the longest expected handler stream (`lambda.Timeout * 2` with a 30s floor — same formula as `invokeRie`, but the absolute value differs because streaming handlers can intentionally run for the full Lambda timeout). Splitting the bound into a strict prelude timer + a per-chunk idle timer that resets on each chunk is deferred to a follow-up (the design discussion lives in [#503](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/503) item 1) — for v1, JSDoc is the contract. (2) **`STREAM_BODY_MAX_BYTES` cap** added at [src/local/rie-client.ts](src/local/rie-client.ts) (100 MiB default, exported alongside the existing `STREAM_PRELUDE_MAX_BYTES = 1 MiB`). Defense-in-depth against a buggy / malicious handler streaming gigabytes — Node's chunked-pipe machinery handles per-chunk backpressure, but the cumulative in-flight buffer can still grow without bound on a slow consumer. The body-drain IIFE tracks cumulative bytes pushed into the Readable; on cap-exceeded it cancels the underlying reader and destroys the Readable with a clear `RIE streaming body exceeded N bytes — destroying stream.` error so the http-server's `'error'` handler runs the same socket-destroy + pool-release path it would for any other mid-stream failure. (3) **`Content-Length` / `Transfer-Encoding` strip on prelude headers** at [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) `writeStreamingResponse` — some handlers set these defensively in `awslambda.HttpResponseStream.from(stream, {headers: ...})` (mistakenly thinking they need to declare the encoding), but a stale Content-Length doesn't match the actual chunked-body bytes and Node either rejects the response synchronously or emits a corrupted Content-Length-but-actually-chunked wire response. The strip is case-insensitive (both `Content-Length` AND `content-length`); Node automatically emits `Transfer-Encoding: chunked` when no Content-Length is set, which is what streaming Function URLs always want. Sibling headers (`Content-Type`, cookies, custom `X-*` headers) pass through intact. Tests: 1 new in [tests/unit/local/rie-client-streaming.test.ts](tests/unit/local/rie-client-streaming.test.ts) (asserts the body Readable destroys with the cap-exceeded error when ≥ 100 MiB + 64 KiB of body bytes arrive); 2 new in [tests/unit/local/http-server.test.ts](tests/unit/local/http-server.test.ts) (PascalCase strip + mixed-case strip + sibling-header preservation + `Transfer-Encoding: chunked` still emitted by Node automatically).

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-service <Stack/Service>` — Phase 2 of [#262](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/262) (closes [#466](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/466) for the service-runner + replica-pool scope; local LB emulator + `--watch` deferred to follow-ups per the issue's PR-split). Long-running ECS Service emulator: discovers an `AWS::ECS::Service`, chains into the existing `cdkd local run-task` machinery, spins up `DesiredCount` task replicas (clamped by `--max-tasks <n>`, default 3), and keeps each replica running until `^C`. Per replica gets its own docker network + AWS-published metadata sidecar via the existing `ecs-network.ts` lifecycle. Restart-on-exit policy via `--restart-policy <on-failure|always|none>` (default `on-failure`): non-zero exits trigger a restart with exponential backoff (1s → 30s capped); `none` runs the service degraded (the affected replica stays down). New modules: [src/local/ecs-service-resolver.ts](src/local/ecs-service-resolver.ts) (synth template → `ResolvedEcsService` carrying DesiredCount / HealthCheckGracePeriodSeconds / underlying `ResolvedEcsTask`; rejects non-`Ref` `TaskDefinition` shapes; warns when `LoadBalancers` / `ServiceConnectConfiguration` are present since both are deferred), [src/local/ecs-service-runner.ts](src/local/ecs-service-runner.ts) (`startEcsService` + `ServiceController.shutdown` long-running orchestrator; per-replica watcher loop with `docker wait` + restart decision; idempotent fan-out shutdown via the shared `singleFlight(...)` helper at [src/utils/single-flight.ts](src/utils/single-flight.ts) — both `ServiceController.shutdown()` AND the CLI's outer-finally `cleanup()` route through it so a SIGTERM-during-outer-finally collapses to one underlying invocation; the controller additionally awaits every in-flight `bootReplica()` promise (tracked per-replica on `ServiceReplicaInstance.inFlightBoot`) BEFORE iterating `instance.state` for cleanup, closing the SIGTERM-mid-restart race where the watcher's `instance.state = createEcsRunState()` + still-in-flight `bootReplica()` would otherwise let cleanup run against an empty state while the boot populated docker network + sidecar handles nobody tracked). The per-replica subnet allocator (`170 + (index % 84)`) caps usable replicas at 84 link-local /24s; the CLI's `parseMaxTasks` rejects `--max-tasks > 84` at parse time with the offending range named so the user sees an actionable error rather than the cryptic Docker "Pool overlaps with other one" failure that would otherwise fire at replica 84, and [src/cli/commands/local-start-service.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-service.ts) (CLI command — mirrors the `local-run-task` flag set minus `--detach` / `--keep-running` since services are long-running; same `--assume-task-role` / `--ecr-role-arn` / `--from-state` plumbing). Registered under the `cdkd local` parent in [src/cli/commands/local-invoke.ts](src/cli/commands/local-invoke.ts). New `LocalStartServiceError` class in [src/utils/error-handler.ts](src/utils/error-handler.ts). **Deferred to follow-up PRs** (per issue [#466](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/466)'s own PR-split recommendation): local load-balancer emulator (listener + target-group health-check + round-robin), `--watch` hot-reload, and Service Connect / Cloud Map (tracked separately in [#460](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/460)). **`awsvpc` decision** documented at [docs/design/461-awsvpc-decision.md](docs/design/461-awsvpc-decision.md) (closes [#461](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/461) at Outcome C — bridge-fallback gap documented; ENI-per-task emulation and security-group emulation are out of scope, matching the precedent set by `cdkd local start-api` VPC simulation in [#234](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/234)). Tests: 16 resolver unit tests + 17 runner unit tests + 12 CLI unit tests across [tests/unit/local/ecs-service-resolver.test.ts](tests/unit/local/ecs-service-resolver.test.ts) / [tests/unit/local/ecs-service-runner.test.ts](tests/unit/local/ecs-service-runner.test.ts) / [tests/unit/cli/local-start-service.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/local-start-service.test.ts). Real-Docker (no AWS deploy) integ at [tests/integration/local-start-service/](tests/integration/local-start-service/) deploys a 2-replica busybox heartbeat service, asserts both replicas reach `docker ps` + each gets its own docker network + metadata sidecar, then SIGTERMs cdkd and asserts every container + network is gone. New `local-ecs-service` scenario tag added to [scripts/build-scenario-coverage-matrix.ts](scripts/build-scenario-coverage-matrix.ts).

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-api` Function URL `InvokeMode: RESPONSE_STREAM` support (closes [#467](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/467)). Pre-PR every `lambda.FunctionUrl` with `invokeMode: lambda.InvokeMode.RESPONSE_STREAM` was rejected at route discovery — the route appeared as `[501 Not Implemented]` and HTTP 501 was returned at request time. Streaming Lambda is increasingly common for AI / LLM proxy endpoints (token-by-token responses), large-file downloads, and any handler where the first byte should ship before the full response is assembled; users could not exercise these locally without a real-AWS deploy. Post-PR cdkd dispatches `RESPONSE_STREAM` routes via the RIE streaming protocol: the request goes out with the `Lambda-Runtime-Function-Response-Mode: streaming` header, RIE returns a response body shaped as `<JSON prelude>` + 8 NULL bytes (`\0\0\0\0\0\0\0\0`) + `<raw body chunks>`, the new helper `parseStreamingPrelude` extracts `{statusCode, headers, cookies?}` from the prefix, and the http-server pipes the body Readable into `res.writeHead(...)` + `body.pipe(res)` so the client sees `Transfer-Encoding: chunked`. Verified empirically against `public.ecr.aws/lambda/nodejs:20` RIE on 2026-05-22 (8-NULL separator, prelude as canonical JSON). **Implementation**: new `invokeRieStreaming` + `parseStreamingPrelude` exports in [src/local/rie-client.ts](src/local/rie-client.ts) (the helper splits the response stream at the separator, drains the post-separator bytes from the current chunk, and returns the remaining `Readable` for the http-server to pipe). [src/local/route-discovery.ts](src/local/route-discovery.ts) `discoverFunctionUrl` drops the `RESPONSE_STREAM === unsupported` branch and tags the route with `invokeMode: 'BUFFERED' | 'RESPONSE_STREAM'`; templates with an unknown InvokeMode value (defensive) still surface a deferred-501 with the offending value named. [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) branches on `match.route.invokeMode === 'RESPONSE_STREAM'` before the buffered `invokeRie` call; the new `writeStreamingResponse` helper writes the prelude's headers + cookies via `res.writeHead`, then pipes the body Readable with full Node backpressure handling and ownership of the pool release (deferred until the body's `'close'` or `'error'` event so the warm container is returned exactly once). Cookies in the prelude are emitted as multiple `Set-Cookie` headers (matches the buffered path's HTTP API v2 semantics). On streaming-invoke failure BEFORE any headers go out, the existing 502 path runs and the pool is released synchronously. **RIE buffers the response** — verified empirically: the v1.0 RIE shipped in `public.ecr.aws/lambda/nodejs:20` does NOT incrementally write the streaming body; it accumulates every `responseStream.write(...)` and emits the whole response as one block when the handler returns, so curl observes ttfb ≈ ttotal locally even though cdkd's pipe / chunked-encoding machinery works correctly. Real incremental delivery only manifests against the deployed Lambda runtime. The integ assertions cover protocol shape (status code, `Transfer-Encoding: chunked` header, prelude-derived response headers, all body chunks intact, no separator bytes leaked into the body) — NOT inter-chunk timing. Tests: 17 new unit tests in [tests/unit/local/rie-client-streaming.test.ts](tests/unit/local/rie-client-streaming.test.ts) covering the prelude parser (statusCode coercion / cookies array / null-header drop / non-object reject) and `invokeRieStreaming` end-to-end against a tiny streaming HTTP server (no Docker — node:http with `res.write` calls + an 8-NULL separator) for happy path / split-prelude-across-chunks / same-chunk-tail-as-body / empty-body / unterminated-prelude / invalid-JSON-prelude / streaming-header-on-request / event-body-forwarding. 5 new tests in [tests/unit/local/route-discovery.test.ts](tests/unit/local/route-discovery.test.ts) (RESPONSE_STREAM normal-route tagging / default BUFFERED / explicit BUFFERED preservation / unknown-mode 501 / regression of the existing NONE-auth assertion with the new `invokeMode: 'BUFFERED'` shape). 4 new tests in [tests/unit/local/http-server.test.ts](tests/unit/local/http-server.test.ts) (RESPONSE_STREAM → invokeRieStreaming + Transfer-Encoding: chunked + body integrity; multiple Set-Cookie from prelude.cookies; BUFFERED falls back to invokeRie; 502 + pool-release on streaming-invoke throw). Integ at [tests/integration/local-start-api/](tests/integration/local-start-api/) extended with a `StreamUrlHandler` Function URL backed by an ESM handler using `awslambda.streamifyResponse` + `awslambda.HttpResponseStream.from` — verify.sh boots the multi-API server, identifies the streaming server's port by the `(StreamUrlHandler<hash> (Function URL))` displayName regex, and asserts the protocol-shape contract above.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-api` dispatches HTTP API v2 service integrations (`IntegrationSubtype`, closes [#458](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/458)). Pre-PR every route with `IntegrationSubtype` set fell through to deferred-501 (`src/local/route-discovery.ts` rejection block); apps that wired routes directly to SQS / EventBridge / Step Functions / Kinesis via HTTP API v2's parameter-mapping integrations had to deploy to AWS just to exercise them locally. Post-PR cdkd recognizes every AWS-documented subtype from <https://docs.aws.amazon.com/apigateway/latest/developerguide/http-api-develop-integrations-aws-services-reference.html> and dispatches each one to the matching AWS SDK call. **Subtypes cdkd currently bundles SDK clients for** (NOT exhaustive — the full AWS-documented list at <https://docs.aws.amazon.com/apigateway/latest/developerguide/http-api-develop-integrations-aws-services-reference.html> also covers `Lambda-Invoke`, the `DynamoDB-*` family, `SNS-Publish`, `AppConfig-StartConfigurationSession`, `SQS-SendMessageBatch`, `Kinesis-PutRecords`, etc.): `EventBridge-PutEvents`, `SQS-SendMessage` / `SQS-ReceiveMessage` / `SQS-DeleteMessage` / `SQS-PurgeQueue`, `Kinesis-PutRecord`, `StepFunctions-StartExecution` / `StartSyncExecution` / `StopExecution`, `AppConfig-GetConfiguration` (recognized but returns 501 — `@aws-sdk/client-appconfig` is not bundled; opt-in follow-up). Unrecognized subtypes (typos AND AWS-documented subtypes cdkd does not yet implement) fall back to the existing deferred-501 path so future-AWS additions still surface as a clean 501 at request time rather than hard-failing boot. **Parameter mapping** ([src/local/parameter-mapping.ts](src/local/parameter-mapping.ts)) is a pure-functional resolver covering the full selection-expression grammar from <https://docs.aws.amazon.com/apigateway/latest/developerguide/http-api-parameter-mapping.html>: `$request.header.<name>` (case-insensitive, multi-value comma-joined), `$request.querystring.<key>` (case-sensitive), `$request.path` / `$request.path.<param>`, `$request.body` / `$request.body.<jsonpath>` (recursive descent `..` and filter `?()` rejected as documented unsupported), `$context.<key>` (cdkd populates `requestId` / `accountId` / `domainName` / `identity.sourceIp` / `httpMethod` / `path` / `protocol` / `requestTime` / `requestTimeEpoch` / `apiId` / `stage`), `$stageVariables.<key>`. Both bare-form (`$request.querystring.url`) and `${...}` interpolation are supported. Unresolved references degrade to `""` (matches AWS-deployed behavior — absent values pass through to the SDK call as empty strings, and the SDK's typed input validator surfaces the error). **Per-subtype dispatcher** ([src/local/httpv2-service-integration.ts](src/local/httpv2-service-integration.ts)) lazy-loads each SDK client (`@aws-sdk/client-sqs` / `client-eventbridge` / `client-kinesis` / `client-sfn`) per-region with a module-level cache, then translates the resolved parameter map into the typed `*Command` input. Per-subtype adapters handle SDK-quirks (Kinesis `Data` is base64-decoded when it matches the base64 alphabet, otherwise treated as UTF-8 bytes; SFN snake_case `StateMachineArn` → camelCase `stateMachineArn`; EventBridge `Resources` CSV → string array; SQS optional `MessageAttributes` JSON-string → object map). **`Region`** is documented on every subtype as the optional SDK-client region override; cdkd resolves the per-request value with fallback to the server's `defaultRegion` (resolved from `--region` / `AWS_REGION` / `AWS_DEFAULT_REGION` at boot). Absent both → 400 with a clear "no region configured" message. **Authentication**: SDK calls run under the dev's local AWS credential chain — no separate `--service-integration-role` flag in this PR (matches the safe-by-default precedent set by `sigv4-verify.ts`; the dev's permissions control what the local route can reach). **Response shape**: each SDK response is JSON-serialized (with `$metadata` stripped) and returned as `200 application/json`. SDK errors are translated to HTTP 4xx / 5xx via `$metadata.httpStatusCode` with `{message, code}` body — the dispatcher never throws. **`ResponseParameters` overlay** is supported per <https://docs.aws.amazon.com/apigateway/latest/developerguide/http-api-parameter-mapping.html#transforming-api-responses>: per-status-code keys `overwrite:statuscode` / `overwrite:header.<name>` / `append:header.<name>` / `remove:header.<name>` with `$context.<X>` / `$stageVariables.<X>` / `$response.header.<name>` value references. Reserved headers (per AWS docs — `content-length`, `connection`, `authorization`, `access-control-*`, `apigw-*`, `x-amz-*`, etc.) are silently skipped at the overlay layer. The `'default'` overlay applies when the exact status code has no entry. **Out of scope (deferred)**: authorizer-protected service-integration routes (the auth pass is currently bypassed for `serviceIntegration` routes — `cdkd local start-api` emits a one-line boot warn naming every affected route via `warnIgnoredServiceIntegrationAuthorizers` so users discover the gap before reaching for AWS; tracked under [#502](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/502)); per-route IAM role assumption (covered by the dev's local credential chain for v1); `$response.body.<jsonpath>` overlay references (would require parsing SDK responses into a uniform shape). Implementation across [src/local/parameter-mapping.ts](src/local/parameter-mapping.ts) (NEW), [src/local/httpv2-service-integration.ts](src/local/httpv2-service-integration.ts) (NEW, ~600 LOC), [src/local/route-discovery.ts](src/local/route-discovery.ts) (new `serviceIntegration` field on `DiscoveredRoute` + `classifyServiceIntegrationRoute` helper), [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) (dispatch branch + `handleServiceIntegrationRequest` + per-request context builder), [src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts](src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts) (skip authorizer attach on service-integration routes — deferred follow-up), [src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts) (`defaultRegion` plumb-through + `uniqueLambdaIds` filter + route-table `[<subtype>]` label). Tests: 24 new in [tests/unit/local/parameter-mapping.test.ts](tests/unit/local/parameter-mapping.test.ts) (every selection-expression form + `${...}` interpolation + JSONPath edge cases + unresolved → "" + malformed-template rejection); 21 new in [tests/unit/local/httpv2-service-integration.test.ts](tests/unit/local/httpv2-service-integration.test.ts) (each supported subtype's SDK input mapping + region resolution + SDK-error → HTTP-4xx translation + `ResponseParameters` overlay matrix including `append:` / `overwrite:` / `remove:` / `default` / reserved-header skip / `${...}` interpolation); 4 new in [tests/unit/local/route-discovery.test.ts](tests/unit/local/route-discovery.test.ts) (classifier emits `serviceIntegration` on recognized subtype / preserves `ResponseParameters` / falls back to deferred-501 on unrecognized subtype / rejects missing-RequestParameters as deferred-501). Integration test extension at [tests/integration/local-start-api/](tests/integration/local-start-api/): fixture stack adds `POST /sqs` (`SQS-SendMessage`), `POST /events` (`EventBridge-PutEvents`), and `POST /unknown-subtype` (obviously-bogus `BogusService-NotASubtype`) via `apigwv2.CfnIntegration` + `apigwv2.CfnRoute` L1; verify.sh asserts (a) the route table surfaces `[SQS-SendMessage]` / `[EventBridge-PutEvents]` labels, (b) `POST /sqs` / `POST /events` return non-501 (proving SDK dispatch fires — typically 4xx from `NonExistentQueue` / `AccessDenied` against the fixture-stable role ARN since no deploy happened), (c) `POST /unknown-subtype` returns 501 with the offending subtype name in the body.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-api` REST v1 non-AWS_PROXY integrations (closes [#457](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/457)). Pre-PR the discovery layer surfaced every non-AWS_PROXY REST v1 integration type (`AWS` Lambda non-proxy, `HTTP`, `HTTP_PROXY`, `MOCK` outside the synthetic CORS-preflight subset) as a deferred-501 unsupported route — boot proceeded but the route returned `HTTP 501 + {"message": "Not Implemented", "reason": ...}` at request time. CDK apps mixing `apigw.LambdaIntegration({proxy: false, ...})` / `apigw.HttpIntegration` / `apigw.MockIntegration` with API Gateway REST v1 couldn't exercise their full surface locally. Post-PR the four non-AWS_PROXY integration kinds are dispatched end-to-end against AWS API Gateway's contract. **Per-integration kind**: (a) **MOCK** (non-CORS) — evaluates `Integration.RequestTemplates['application/json']` (VTL) to extract the `{"statusCode": N}` selection driver, matches it against `IntegrationResponses[].StatusCode`, then renders the picked `ResponseTemplates[<content-type>]` (VTL) against an empty input context with `$inputRoot = null`. Apply `ResponseParameters` header literals. (b) **HTTP_PROXY** — forward the HTTP request to `Integration.Uri` (with `{paramName}` path-placeholder substitution from the matched route's pathParameters), honor `Integration.IntegrationHttpMethod` override, propagate request headers minus hop-by-hop (`host` / `connection` / `content-length` / `transfer-encoding`), apply `Integration.RequestParameters` mappings (`integration.request.header.X = method.request.header.Y` / `= 'literal'` form supported; querystring / path mappings recognized but logged-and-skipped since `{param}` URI substitution handles the canonical case), forward the upstream response verbatim with `IntegrationResponses[].SelectionPattern` (regex against the upstream status as a string) driving the final HTTP status. (c) **HTTP** (non-proxy) — HTTP_PROXY + bidirectional VTL: `RequestTemplates` transforms the body before sending upstream; `IntegrationResponses[].ResponseTemplates` transforms the upstream body before returning. (d) **AWS** (Lambda non-proxy) — VTL request template synthesizes the Lambda event payload (parsed as JSON when the rendered template is valid JSON, otherwise passed through verbatim — matches AWS-deployed behavior), invokes the Lambda via the existing warm RIE container pool, detects the Lambda error envelope (`{errorMessage, errorType?, stackTrace?}` shape Node Lambda runtime emits) and routes through `SelectionPattern` regex matched against `errorMessage`, finally renders the picked entry's response template with `$inputRoot = <parsed Lambda payload>`. **Direct AWS-service integrations** (`Integration.Type: 'AWS'` with Uri pointing at `:s3:path/...` / `:sqs:action/...` / etc.) are detected via the Lambda invoke-path marker (`:lambda:path/2015-03-31/functions/`) and surface as deferred-501 unsupported routes with a clear "non-Lambda service ... not emulated locally in cdkd v1" reason. **Hand-rolled minimal VTL evaluator** at [src/local/vtl-engine.ts](src/local/vtl-engine.ts) — no external dependency added. Supported subset: variable references (`$var` / `${var}` / `$obj.field.subField`), method calls on built-ins (`$input.body` / `$input.json('$.path')` / `$input.path('$.path')` / `$input.params(...)` / `$context.*` / `$util.escapeJavaScript` / `$util.base64Encode` / `$util.base64Decode` / `$util.urlEncode` / `$util.urlDecode` / `$util.parseJson`), `#set` / `#if` / `#elseif` / `#else` / `#end` / `#foreach` / `##` comment directives, logical operators (`&&` / `||` / `!`), comparison operators (`==` / `!=` / `<` / `<=` / `>` / `>=`), string / number / boolean / null literals. JSONPath is a minimal subset (`$`, `$.field`, `$.field.sub`, `$.array[index]`, quoted-string bracket keys); filter expressions (`$..items`) hard-reject with a clear pointer at the gap. Velocity arithmetic operators (`+ - * /`), user-defined macros (`#macro`), `#parse` / `#include`, the `[1..5]` range syntax, and `$velocityCount` are intentionally NOT supported — any usage surfaces `VtlEvaluationError` with the offending construct named. VTL evaluation failures route to HTTP 502 with the template + reason in the JSON body so users see exactly what failed without an opaque 500. **IntegrationResponses[] selection** at [src/local/integration-response-selector.ts](src/local/integration-response-selector.ts) — `SelectionPattern` regex is anchored with `^...$` (matches AWS-deployed behavior); the regex loop ALWAYS runs, even for upstream-success outcomes, so a `SelectionPattern: '200'` entry actually matches a 200 upstream response (the pre-PR-#505-review draft short-circuited the success branch to the default entry without running the regex loop, which silently dropped success-side selection). Invalid regex in a template is skipped (rather than aborting the whole dispatch) so a typo doesn't make the route un-emulatable; the AWS-doc-canonical fall-back-to-default-entry semantics on no-match apply. `evaluateResponseParameters` extracts single-quoted literal header values (`"'literal'"`) and warn-and-skips mapping expressions (`integration.response.body.X` / `context.X`); v1 only supports the literal form. `pickResponseTemplate` does Accept-header content negotiation, falling back to `application/json` then any first entry. **Dispatch order**: per-request the http-server runs the authorizer pass FIRST (so a Lambda authorizer / Cognito JWT guards MOCK / HTTP / AWS Lambda non-proxy routes too), then the integration dispatcher. The container pool is consulted ONLY for AWS Lambda non-proxy routes; MOCK / HTTP / HTTP_PROXY add zero container-acquire overhead. The CLI's `uniqueLambdaIds` already correctly skips routes with `lambdaLogicalId === ''`, so non-Lambda integration kinds don't allocate containers. **Body forwarding** on HTTP_PROXY / HTTP is gated on `req.body.length > 0` (NOT on HTTP method) so an integration that overrides the upstream method to GET via `IntegrationHttpMethod` still forwards the client body — closes a PR #505 review minor. `content-length` is stripped from forwarded headers regardless (fetch recomputes it from `body`). **`content-encoding` strip on HTTP_PROXY upstream**: `fetch` auto-decodes gzip / deflate / br on the upstream Response and the body reaches cdkd as plaintext; cdkd strips `content-encoding` AND `content-length` from the forwarded response headers so downstream clients do not double-decode or trust a stale encoded byte count. **HTTP non-proxy binary upstream**: the dispatcher branches on the upstream `Content-Type` — text-like types (`text/*`, `application/json`, `application/xml`, `application/javascript`, `application/ld+json`, `application/*+json`, `application/*+xml`, `application/x-www-form-urlencoded`) are decoded as UTF-8 strings so VTL ResponseTemplates can run; other types pass through as a Buffer (no UTF-8 corruption). A ResponseTemplate against a binary upstream warns-and-passes-through the binary unchanged. **SSRF warning at boot**: every HTTP / HTTP_PROXY integration's `Integration.Uri` is classified at server boot; hostnames matching AWS IMDS (`169.254.169.254`), IPv4 / IPv6 loopback, link-local, or RFC1918 emit a deduplicated `logger.warn` line per URI naming the destination class. cdkd does NOT block — warn-and-proceed matches the cognito JWKS pass-through precedent; threading an `--allow-internal-uri` block flag is deferred (this is a developer-loop tool, not a security boundary, and the source URI is the user's own CDK template). **Implementation**: 3 new modules — [src/local/vtl-engine.ts](src/local/vtl-engine.ts) (VTL evaluator + built-in factories), [src/local/integration-response-selector.ts](src/local/integration-response-selector.ts) (selection / response-template / response-parameter helpers; `selectIntegrationResponse(entries, matchTarget, fallbackStatusCode)` signature), [src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts](src/local/rest-v1-integrations.ts) (four dispatcher functions + URI placeholder substitution + RequestParameters mapping + `isTextLikeContentType` + `classifyInternalHost` + `warnSsrfRiskyUri`). [src/local/route-discovery.ts](src/local/route-discovery.ts) gained the new `RestV1IntegrationConfig` discriminated union (`mock` / `http-proxy` / `http` / `aws-lambda`) on `DiscoveredRoute.restV1Integration` and per-kind classification helpers (`buildMockIntegrationConfig` / `buildHttpProxyIntegrationConfig` / `buildHttpIntegrationConfig` / `buildAwsIntegrationConfig` / `readIntegrationResponses`) that pull the integration sub-resource's `RequestTemplates` / `IntegrationResponses[]` / `RequestParameters` / `Uri`. The pre-PR MOCK CORS-preflight extraction (CDK `defaultCorsPreflightOptions` synth shape) runs FIRST as a synthetic preflight route the http-server answers directly; any other MOCK shape (non-OPTIONS, or OPTIONS without the canonical CORS literals) falls through to the full MOCK dispatcher. [src/local/http-server.ts](src/local/http-server.ts) gains a `dispatchRestV1Integration` branch after the authorizer pass that builds a `RestV1IntegrationRequest` snapshot (method / matchedPath / pathParameters / querystring / lowercased headers / body buffer / sourceIp / userAgent / stage / resourcePath / synthesized UUID requestId) and routes to the right dispatcher. [src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts) `printRouteTable` now labels non-AWS_PROXY routes with `[MOCK]` / `[HTTP_PROXY <uri>]` / `[HTTP <uri>]` / `<lambdaId> [AWS]` so the boot output makes the integration kind obvious at a glance; `warnSsrfRiskyIntegrations` runs alongside the unsupported-route warn pass to surface internal-address upstreams. **Out of scope** (deferred to follow-up PRs): direct AWS-service integrations (S3 / SQS / SNS / DynamoDB / Step Functions / etc.) — would require per-service SDK clients, IAM credential threading, and a sizable per-service compatibility matrix. **Tests**: 4 new test files — [tests/unit/local/vtl-engine.test.ts](tests/unit/local/vtl-engine.test.ts) (29 tests: literal text / variable refs / `$input.body` / `$input.json` / `$input.path` / `$input.params` precedence / `$util.*` round-trips / `#set` / `#if` / `#elseif` / `#else` / `#foreach` / `##` comment / `&&` / `||` / `!` / JSONPath positive + negative), [tests/unit/local/integration-response-selector.test.ts](tests/unit/local/integration-response-selector.test.ts) (selector default-entry / regex match / fallback / regex anchoring / invalid regex skip / always-applied regex on success + 2xx wildcard + first-match-wins / literal-header extraction / mapping-expression skip / Accept-header content negotiation), [tests/unit/local/rest-v1-integrations.test.ts](tests/unit/local/rest-v1-integrations.test.ts) (MOCK status-code selection / ResponseParameters / VTL failure / HTTP_PROXY upstream forwarding / placeholder substitution / unreachable upstream → 502 / SelectionPattern status routing on success + on error / body-forwarding-gate matrix / content-encoding strip / text-vs-binary upstream branching / 16-case Content-Type matrix / HTTP non-proxy request + response VTL / AWS Lambda non-proxy with request + response VTL / errorMessage routing / container-acquire failure / substituteUriPlaceholders edge cases / SSRF classification matrix for IMDS / loopback / link-local / RFC1918 / public DNS / 172.16-172.31 boundary), and 7 new positive route-discovery tests in [tests/unit/local/route-discovery.test.ts](tests/unit/local/route-discovery.test.ts) (each of the 4 supported kinds → restV1Integration populated; non-Lambda AWS service → unsupported; HTTP_PROXY non-literal Uri → unsupported; unknown Type → unsupported). Three pre-PR tests asserting "MOCK is unsupported" updated to assert the new `kind: 'mock'` classification. Real-Docker integ at [tests/integration/local-start-api-rest-v1-non-proxy/](tests/integration/local-start-api-rest-v1-non-proxy/) deploys nothing and exercises four routes end-to-end against `public.ecr.aws/lambda/nodejs:20`: `GET /mock-200` (MOCK + request-template-driven 200 + response-template literal), `GET /mock-404` (MOCK + request-template-driven 404 + response-template error body), `GET /http-proxy` (HTTP_PROXY to `https://httpbin.org/get` — tolerant of network-isolated CI: accepts 200 OR 502), `POST /aws-lambda` (AWS Lambda non-proxy with request-side VTL extracting `action` / `name` from the body + response-side VTL wrapping `$input.json("$.greeting")` into `{"data": ...}`). Verify.sh asserts the round-tripped Lambda response shows both the request-VTL-extracted name AND the response-VTL-wrapped envelope. PR title format `(#457)` (per the pr-body-item-number-gate hook); no body file references with bare `#N` patterns.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd export` and `cdkd import --migrate-from-cloudformation` accept YAML templates (closes [#452](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/452)). Both directions of CFn migration go through a new CFn-aware codec at [src/cli/yaml-cfn.ts](src/cli/yaml-cfn.ts) that preserves every CFn shorthand intrinsic across the parse → mutate → re-serialize round-trip. Tags supported: `!Ref`, `!GetAtt` (both `LogicalId.Attribute` scalar and `[LogicalId, Attribute]` sequence shapes), `!Sub`, `!Join`, `!Select`, `!Split`, `!If`, `!Equals`, `!And`, `!Or`, `!Not`, `!FindInMap`, `!Base64`, `!Cidr`, `!GetAZs`, `!ImportValue`, `!Transform`, `!Condition`, `!Length`, `!ToJsonString`, `!ForEach`. Each `!Foo` parses to the long-form `{Fn::Foo: <args>}` object (or `{Ref: <name>}` for `!Ref`) so every downstream consumer (`injectRetainPolicies`, `executeImportChangeSet`, `executeUpdateChangeSet`) reads one canonical representation, and re-serializes back to the same shorthand tag on YAML emit. Format auto-detection sniffs the first non-whitespace byte of the input text (after stripping any UTF-8 BOM): `{` or `[` → JSON; anything else → YAML (matches CDK CLI's [`serialize.ts`](https://github.com/aws/aws-cdk-cli)). The detected format flows through the entire emit chain — a YAML-authored CFn stack stays YAML on the phase-1 IMPORT and phase-2 UPDATE changesets, and on the transient S3 upload that backs templates over the 51,200-byte inline limit (`.yaml` key suffix + `application/x-yaml` content type when the source was YAML; `.json` + `application/json` otherwise). Built on the `yaml` package (`eemeli/yaml`, 0 runtime deps) which exposes the per-tag customTags resolver hook the codec needs; each tag is registered three times (scalar / seq / map) to match the `yaml` library's per-shape resolver contract. Nested intrinsics resolve recursively via `node.toJSON()` (the yaml lib resolves child customTags before invoking the parent's resolver), so a `!Join [':', ['arn', !Ref AWS::Region]]` round-trips cleanly to `{Fn::Join: [':', ['arn', {Ref: 'AWS::Region'}]]}`. Malformed `!GetAtt` without a dot (e.g. `!GetAtt LogicalIdOnly`) is rejected at parse time with a clear error rather than silently producing `{Fn::GetAtt: ['LogicalIdOnly', '']}`. **Implementation**: new module `src/cli/yaml-cfn.ts` exporting `parseCfnTemplate(text)` + `parseCfnTemplateWithFormat(text)` + `stringifyCfnTemplate(template, format)` + `detectTemplateFormat(text)` + `detectTemplateFormatByPath(path)` + the `TemplateFormat = 'json' | 'yaml'` type alias. `injectRetainPolicies()` in [src/cli/commands/retire-cfn-stack.ts](src/cli/commands/retire-cfn-stack.ts) widened to return `{body, modified, format}` (was `{body, modified}`); `uploadTemplateForUpdateStack()` gains an optional `format` argument that controls the S3 key extension + content type. `executeImportChangeSet()` / `executeUpdateChangeSet()` in [src/cli/commands/export.ts](src/cli/commands/export.ts) gain an optional `templateFormat` argument (defaults to `'json'` for the CDK-synth path); the `--template <path>` branch routes through `parseCfnTemplateWithFormat()` so a user-supplied YAML template threads its format all the way to the CFn API. **Tests**: unit tests in [tests/unit/cli/yaml-cfn.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/yaml-cfn.test.ts) covering every tag's per-shape resolver (including `!Length` / `!ToJsonString` / `!ForEach` + per-tag stringify round-trip for `!Sub` / `!Select` / `!Split` / `!If` / `!Equals` / `!And` / `!Or` / `!Not` / `!FindInMap` / `!Base64` / `!Cidr` / `!GetAZs` / `!ImportValue`), round-trip stability on a 17-tag fixture, BOM-prefixed JSON detection, dot-less `!GetAtt` rejection, plus a real-world CDK-synthesized YAML fixture. Updates in [tests/unit/cli/export.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/export.test.ts) verify `templateFormat: 'yaml'` plumbs through to `CreateChangeSetCommand.TemplateBody` on both `executeImportChangeSet` and `executeUpdateChangeSet`, and that `parseTemplateFile` routes YAML files through the YAML codec. Updates in [tests/unit/cli/retire-cfn-stack.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/retire-cfn-stack.test.ts) cover the small-YAML inline path AND the large-YAML S3 upload path with `.yaml` key suffix + `application/x-yaml` content type. The `yaml` package is the only new runtime dep added (~80kB, 0 transitive runtime deps). Docs updated: [docs/import.md](docs/import.md) "Limitations" section flipped from JSON-only to JSON-and-YAML with a one-paragraph note on the CFn-aware codec.

- ✅ `Fn::GetStackOutput` cross-account `RoleArn` support (closes [#449](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/449)). Pre-PR `src/deployment/intrinsic-function-resolver.ts` rejected any `RoleArn` argument with the "not yet supported" error, blocking the canonical multi-account pattern (shared-services account producing platform outputs consumed by workload accounts). Post-PR cdkd assumes the supplied role and reads the producer account's separate cdkd state bucket end-to-end: (1) parse `RoleArn` via the new `parseIamRoleArn(arn)` helper in [src/utils/role-arn.ts](src/utils/role-arn.ts) (regex accepts every published AWS partition — `aws` / `aws-us-gov` / `aws-cn` / `aws-iso*` — and any role-name path shape including service-linked-role prefixes; rejects non-IAM ARNs, IAM user ARNs, and non-12-digit account IDs up front); (2) `sts:AssumeRole` via the new `assumeRoleForCrossAccountStateRead(roleArn)` helper, which caches the resulting `AwsCredentials` per role-ARN for the deploy lifetime (a multi-resource stack with N `Fn::GetStackOutput` sites against the same producer pays exactly one STS hop) and stores the in-flight `Promise` to collapse concurrent first-time callers; (3) derive the producer's canonical state bucket name (`cdkd-state-{producerAccountId}`) and auto-detect its region via the new `resolveCrossAccountStateBucket(accountId, credentials)` helper in [src/utils/aws-region-resolver.ts](src/utils/aws-region-resolver.ts) — `GetBucketLocation` reuses the existing `resolveBucketRegion()` per-bucket cache, threaded with the assumed credentials so the producer's bucket policy authorizes against the assumed principal; (4) construct a fresh, narrowly-scoped `S3Client` + `S3StateBackend` against the producer's bucket and call `getState(stackName, region)` — reuses the full state-parsing + schema-version-tolerance machinery (legacy v1 keys, migration warnings, region key layout). The cross-account branch is structurally separate from the same-account branch (split into `getCrossAccountStackState(...)` and `getSameAccountStackState(...)` helpers on the resolver) so the same-account path stays uncluttered. **The inline `RoleArn` argument is constrained to LITERAL strings only** — `Ref` / `Fn::GetAtt` / `Fn::Sub` chains are rejected with a clear "RoleArn must be a literal string in the template" error before any STS call fires; the resolver context cannot guarantee producer-account info at intrinsic-resolution time and a typo'd role lookup is far worse than a clear template-author-time error. **No `process.env` mutation**: unlike the CLI-wide `--role-arn` flag (which writes assumed creds into `AWS_*` env vars so every later SDK client picks them up), the cross-account path threads credentials only into the ephemeral S3 state-backend client — the consumer's normal provisioning credentials are untouched. Same-account references (no RoleArn) take the original shared-state-backend path with no behavior change. Self-reference detection skips the cross-account branch (a producer with the same stack name + region in a different account is by definition not self-reference). 18 new unit tests across [tests/unit/utils/role-arn-cross-account.test.ts](tests/unit/utils/role-arn-cross-account.test.ts) (parser edge cases: aws-us-gov / aws-cn / service-linked-role path / IAM user rejection / non-12-digit account ID / cache reuse / process.env isolation / concurrent caller collapse) and [tests/unit/deployment/intrinsic-getstackoutput-cross-account.test.ts](tests/unit/deployment/intrinsic-getstackoutput-cross-account.test.ts) (intrinsic-shape rejection for `Ref` / `Fn::Sub` / empty / malformed / IAM user ARN; happy path with STS + GetBucketLocation + GetObject mocked; cache reuse across multiple resolves; bucket region auto-detection independent of consumer region; not-found error names the cross-account context; aws-us-gov partition end-to-end; same-account regression preserved; cross-account NOT treated as self-reference even when stack name + region match). Implementation: [src/utils/role-arn.ts](src/utils/role-arn.ts) (new `AwsCredentials` interface + `parseIamRoleArn` + `assumeRoleForCrossAccountStateRead` + `clearCrossAccountCredentialsCache` test helper), [src/utils/aws-region-resolver.ts](src/utils/aws-region-resolver.ts) (new `resolveCrossAccountStateBucket`), [src/deployment/intrinsic-function-resolver.ts](src/deployment/intrinsic-function-resolver.ts) (`resolveGetStackOutput` refactor + `getCrossAccountStackState` / `getSameAccountStackState` helpers + literal-string `RoleArn` constraint at template layer), [docs/cross-stack-references.md](docs/cross-stack-references.md) (caveat removed + new "Cross-account references" section). Cross-account integration test deferred — requires a second AWS account; the issue's test-strategy notes the `CDKD_INTEG_CROSS_ACCOUNT=1` env-gated path as the follow-up.

- ✅ Fix: `DynamoDBGlobalTableProvider.create()` propagates Tags to cross-region replicas (closes [#441](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/441)). Pre-fix `CreateTable.Tags` only covered the LOCAL replica — the `Replicas[].Tags` entries on non-local replicas silently dropped during the initial create, so the first `cdkd drift` against a freshly-created multi-region table reported Tags drift on every cross-region replica (recoverable on the next `cdkd deploy` via the update-path's per-region propagation, but UX-noisy). Post-fix, after each non-local replica flips ACTIVE in `addReplica`, cdkd iterates the replica list again and issues `TagResource` against each replica's region-scoped ARN via the cached per-region `DynamoDBClient` from `getRegionalClient(region)`. The wire layer is the new shared helper `applyCrossRegionReplicaTagsDiff(tableArn, region, oldTags, newTags, physicalIdForLogs)` in [src/provisioning/providers/dynamodb-globaltable-provider.ts](src/provisioning/providers/dynamodb-globaltable-provider.ts), which centralizes the diff (`deepEqual` short-circuit), the ARN-derivation guard via `replicaArnForRegion`, and the best-effort WARN-on-failure contract that BOTH `create()` (oldTags=undefined → every tag is an add) and `update()` (per-replica modify path's old-vs-new diff + the newly-ADDED replica path) now go through. The inline ~30-LOC block in `update()` is replaced with a single helper call — the inline-duplication that Issue #441 called out is gone. Best-effort: a single region's `TagResource` failure logs at WARN naming the region + ARN + reason ("will surface as drift until the next successful deploy") and the deploy continues (matches `update()`'s precedent). The stale "Cross-region replicas require per-region SDK clients [...], deferred to a follow-up PR" docstring on `readCurrentState` is gone, replaced with prose matching the post-Issue #389 reality (per-region readCurrentState already implemented). Class-level docstring updated to point at the shared helper. 4 new unit tests in [tests/unit/provisioning/dynamodb-globaltable-provider-roundtrip.test.ts](tests/unit/provisioning/dynamodb-globaltable-provider-roundtrip.test.ts): (a) cross-region replica Tags propagated via regional TagResource targeting the swapped-region ARN on create, LOCAL replica's Tags still go through `CreateTable.Tags` (preserve fast path), no UntagResource issued (oldTags=undefined on create); (b) non-local replica with no Tags short-circuits the loop — no regional TagResource fires, no regional client spawned; (c) regional TagResource failure logs WARN and the create returns successfully (no abort); (d) update() added-replica path propagates Tags via regional TagResource (closes the parallel bug class on the update side surfaced during code review).

- ✅ Audit + first batch of partially-supported `provider.update()` rejections (closes (#443) for the AppSync batch; follow-ups [#475](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/475) / [#476](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/476) / [#477](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/477) track the rest). **Audit**: walked every `ResourceUpdateNotSupportedError` throw site in `src/provisioning/providers/` and classified each as `architectural` (AWS has no in-place Update API — e.g. ECS TaskDefinition revisions, Lambda LayerVersion, Glue SecurityConfiguration, Kinesis StreamConsumer, EC2 sub-resources, RDS DBProxy family identity fields, ApiGwV2 immutable identity fields, ELBv2 LoadBalancer Name/Type/Scheme, EFS AccessPoint + FileSystem Encrypted/KmsKeyId/PerformanceMode, ASG AutoScalingGroupName, API Gateway Deployment) or `unimplemented` (AWS exposes the API; cdkd just hasn't wired it — AppSync types, ASG Tags / LoadBalancerNames / TargetGroupARNs, Firehose UpdateDestination). 18 of ~22 sites are architectural; 4 implementable groups identified. **AppSync update implementation** (this PR's first implementable batch): [src/provisioning/providers/appsync-provider.ts](src/provisioning/providers/appsync-provider.ts) wires `UpdateGraphqlApi` / `UpdateDataSource` / `UpdateResolver` / `UpdateApiKey` / `StartSchemaCreation` (+ `TagResource` / `UntagResource` for GraphqlApi Tags). Mutable fields use `!== undefined` gates per `feedback_update_optional_field_undefined_check.md`. Immutable identity fields (Name on GraphqlApi, ApiId/Name/Type on DataSource, ApiId/TypeName/FieldName on Resolver, ApiId on ApiKey) throw `ResourceUpdateNotSupportedError` as defense-in-depth. Per-method no-op skip when nothing diffs. Tags diff issues `GetGraphqlApi` to recover the ARN, then `UntagResource` for removed keys + `TagResource` for added / changed keys (skipped entirely when before/after tag maps are deepEqual). **Tightened architectural rejection messages** across the audited sites: every `ResourceUpdateNotSupportedError` thrown for a genuinely-immutable field now names the AWS constraint (e.g. "ECS TaskDefinition revisions are immutable on AWS — there is no UpdateTaskDefinition API; every change registers a new revision via RegisterTaskDefinition") instead of the generic "use --replace" wording. Users no longer need to read source to know which rejections are AWS-side vs cdkd-side. Pure UX change; no behavior delta. The ASG Tags / LoadBalancerNames / TargetGroupARNs rejection messages also got an "unimplemented in cdkd (AWS exposes ...)" tag that points at the follow-up issues. **Tests**: rewrote [tests/unit/provisioning/appsync-provider-roundtrip.test.ts](tests/unit/provisioning/appsync-provider-roundtrip.test.ts) (was a 6-test rejection-asserting file; now 14 update-path tests covering each Update*Command, the no-op-when-unchanged path, `!== undefined` empty-string clearing for DataSource.Description, immutable identity rejection per type, and the GraphqlApi tag-diff GetGraphqlApi → UntagResource → TagResource sequence). Updated the legacy `tests/unit/provisioning/providers/appsync-provider.test.ts` dispatch block to match the new behavior (no blanket rejection at the dispatch layer; immutable identity rejections moved into per-type handlers). Follow-up issues filed: [#475](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/475) (ASG Tags), [#476](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/476) (ASG LoadBalancers + TargetGroups), [#477](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/477) (Firehose UpdateDestination, ExtendedS3 first).

**Recently Implemented** (2026-05-16):

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-api` container image Lambda (`Code.ImageUri`) support (closes [#453](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/453)). Pre-PR the server rejected any Lambda with `Code.ImageUri` at boot with `'cdkd local start-api' v1 supports ZIP Lambdas only — container-image support is deferred to a follow-up PR. Use 'cdkd local invoke' to exercise this function locally.`, so CDK apps mixing `lambda.DockerImageFunction` constructs with API Gateway routes could not run their full surface locally. Post-PR the container-Lambda machinery added in PR 5 of #224 (image asset lookup via `cdk.out/<stack>.assets.json`, `docker build` against the recorded build context, ECR-pull same-acct/region fallback, `--platform` from `Architectures`, `ImageConfig.{Command,EntryPoint,WorkingDirectory}` forwarding) is threaded through `cdkd local start-api`'s warm container pool. **Load-bearing refactor**: `ContainerSpec` in [src/local/container-pool.ts](src/local/container-pool.ts) is now a discriminated union — `ZipContainerSpec` (the original shape: `kind: 'zip'` + `codeDir` + optional `optDir` for /opt layer mount + `lambda: ResolvedZipLambda`) and `ImageContainerSpec` (new: `kind: 'image'` + pre-built local `image` tag + `platform` + `command` / optional `entryPoint` / optional `workingDir` + `lambda: ResolvedImageLambda`). `createContainerPool.startOne` branches on `spec.kind`: ZIP keeps the existing `/var/task` (or `/var/runtime` for `provided.al2*`) bind-mount + `/opt` layer mount path; IMAGE skips all host mounts (image already contains the code), runs the pre-built local tag verbatim, threads `--platform` / `--entrypoint <first>` / `--workdir` / `cmd` through `docker-runner.runDetached` via fields the same module already accepts since PR 5 of #224. **Image build at server boot**: `buildContainerSpec` in [src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts) branches on `lambda.kind` — ZIP runs the existing `materializeInlineCode` + `materializeLambdaLayers` path; IMAGE calls a new `resolveContainerImageForStartApi` helper that mirrors `local-invoke.ts:resolveContainerImagePlan` (local-build via `AssetManifestLoader` + `getDockerImageBySourceHash` + `buildContainerImage` on a cdk.out asset hit, ECR-pull fallback via `parseEcrUri` + `pullEcrImage` when no matching asset is found). The local-build path uses the same deterministic `cdkd-local-invoke-<sha-of-source-dir>` tag from PR 5 of #224 (shared via the `docker-image-builder` module — no separate tag namespace for start-api), so the docker layer cache is reused across `cdkd local invoke` AND `cdkd local start-api` invocations against the same Lambda. **Hot reload (`--watch`)**: `reload-orchestrator.ts:specSignature` was extended to branch on `spec.kind` — ZIP's signature includes `codeDir` / `handler` / `runtime`, IMAGE's signature includes `image` (the deterministic tag, which already content-addresses the build context per `docker-image-builder.ts:computeLocalTag`) / `command` / `entryPoint` / `workingDir` / `platform`. A Dockerfile edit produces a new tag at the next reload's `buildContainerImage` call, the signature change is detected, and the container pool tears down + restarts for the affected Lambda. **Layers silently ignored on IMAGE**: matches AWS's invoke-time behavior — `lambda.DockerImageFunction.Layers` is rejected at deploy time on the AWS side because layers are baked into the image at build time, not overlaid at runtime. `resolveLambdaByLogicalId`'s IMAGE branch sets `layers: []` regardless of the template's `Properties.Layers`. **Pull pass**: `synthesizeAndBuild`'s `distinctImages` loop now filters to `spec.kind === 'zip'` — IMAGE specs already had their per-Lambda image resolved by `buildContainerSpec` before this point, so the pool can `docker run` against it without any further pull step. **Watched-asset list**: `computeAssetPaths` similarly walks only ZIP specs — IMAGE Lambdas have no host-side bind-mount source (code lives inside the image); their build-context-dir watch is deferred to a follow-up (the existing `cdk.out/`-rooted watch transitively covers most container-Lambda asset dirs because `cdk synth` re-stages them). **Out of scope**: cross-account / cross-region ECR pull (same boundary as PR 5 of #224 — tracked separately as the W2-1 follow-up). Implementation across [src/local/container-pool.ts](src/local/container-pool.ts) (discriminated union + branching `startOne`), [src/local/reload-orchestrator.ts](src/local/reload-orchestrator.ts) (kind-aware spec signature), [src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts) (dual-kind `ResolvedStartApiLambda` + `resolveLambdaByLogicalId` IMAGE branch + `buildContainerSpec` IMAGE branch + `resolveContainerImageForStartApi` + `resolveLocalBuildPlan` helpers + pull-loop / asset-paths filtering). Tests: 8 new in [tests/unit/local/container-pool-image.test.ts](tests/unit/local/container-pool-image.test.ts) (IMAGE spec → docker run shape: `spec.image` verbatim, no `/var/task` bind-mount, `--platform` threaded, `ImageConfig.Command` / `EntryPoint` / `WorkingDirectory` forwarded, `debugPort` threaded, `extraMounts` always empty, `resolveRuntimeImage` never consulted on IMAGE branch, ZIP + IMAGE coexist in the same pool); 11 new in [tests/unit/cli/local-start-api-container.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/local-start-api-container.test.ts) (`resolveLambdaByLogicalId` IMAGE branch: flat-string ImageUri / `Fn::Sub` string-form / `Fn::Sub` array-form / arm64 honored / x86_64 default / unsupported architecture rejected / ImageConfig field forwarding / ImageConfig absent → undefined fields / ZIP regression / no Runtime + no ImageUri rejection / Handler missing rejection / no Lambda found rejection); 3 existing test files updated for the new union shape ([container-pool.test.ts](tests/unit/local/container-pool.test.ts), [container-pool-dispose.test.ts](tests/unit/local/container-pool-dispose.test.ts), [reload-orchestrator.test.ts](tests/unit/local/reload-orchestrator.test.ts)). Real-Docker (no AWS deploy) integ at [tests/integration/local-start-api-container/](tests/integration/local-start-api-container/) deploys a single `lambda.DockerImageFunction` + HTTP API v2 `GET /` route, boots the server, asserts the route table contains `GET /`, then curls the route and asserts the container's `fromContainer: true` marker and `greeting: 'hello'` env-var pass-through.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd export` submits CFn change-set templates over the 51,200-byte inline `TemplateBody` ceiling via `TemplateURL` upload up to the 1 MB `TemplateURL` limit (closes [#450](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/450)). Pre-fix every phase-1 IMPORT / phase-2 UPDATE template > 51,200 bytes hard-failed at `executeImportChangeSet` / `executeUpdateChangeSet` (in [src/cli/commands/export.ts](src/cli/commands/export.ts)) with an error pointing at the deferred follow-up — CDK apps with > ~50 resources, nested constructs, or inline Lambda code structurally couldn't export. `cdkd import --migrate-from-cloudformation` had already solved the same wire-format trap for its post-state-write `UpdateStack` via `uploadTemplateForUpdateStack` in [src/cli/commands/retire-cfn-stack.ts](src/cli/commands/retire-cfn-stack.ts); the helper now lives at the new shared module [src/cli/upload-cfn-template.ts](src/cli/upload-cfn-template.ts) (`uploadCfnTemplate(args): {url, cleanup}` + `CFN_TEMPLATE_BODY_LIMIT` / `CFN_TEMPLATE_URL_LIMIT` / `MIGRATE_TMP_PREFIX` / `findLargeInlineResources` constants & helpers) and is consumed by both flows so the operator-facing audit trail (CloudTrail records under `cdkd-migrate-tmp/<stack>/<ts>.{json,yaml}`) and the cleanup contract are single-sourced. `retire-cfn-stack.ts:uploadTemplateForUpdateStack` is kept as a thin pass-through wrapper so existing call sites and tests stay unchanged. **Routing matrix** in `selectChangeSetTemplateSource` (exported from `export.ts` for unit testing): `<= 51_200` → inline `TemplateBody`; `(51_200, 1_048_576]` → `TemplateURL` upload to the cdkd state bucket; `> 1_048_576` → pre-flight refuse with an actionable error naming the heaviest inline-payload contributors (`findLargeInlineResources` walks every resource's `Properties` JSON-size and surfaces the top 10 above the 4096-byte threshold so the user knows what to shrink — typically inline `Code.ZipFile` Lambdas should switch to `lambda.Code.fromAsset(...)`, otherwise template-split via nested `AWS::CloudFormation::Stack` resources). Both `executeImportChangeSet` (phase 1 IMPORT) and `executeUpdateChangeSet` (phase 2 UPDATE) honor the same routing per memory rule `feedback_phase1_phase2_template_symmetry.md` — phase 2 is the more common trigger because it submits the FULL synth template while phase 1 only submits the importable subset; both wrap the wait/execute body in a `try { ... } finally { await runTemplateUploadCleanup(...); }` so the transient S3 object is removed regardless of CFn success / failure (CFn copies the template into internal storage during the synchronous `CreateChangeSet` call, so the S3 object is no longer needed once `CreateChangeSet` returns). Cleanup failures are best-effort: `runTemplateUploadCleanup` logs at WARN with the recovery prefix `cdkd-migrate-tmp/` so a stranded object is easy to reap manually and never blocks the calling command (mirrors the existing `retireCloudFormationStack` warn pattern). The new `ChangeSetUploadOpts` struct carries `{stateBucket, s3ClientOpts?}` and is threaded from the `runExport` body which already resolved `stateBucket` via `resolveStateBucketWithDefault` for the lock manager — no new CLI flag needed. The transient upload's `.json` / `.yaml` key suffix + `application/json` / `application/x-yaml` Content-Type mirrors the source template format (composes with the YAML support added in the matching `--migrate-from-cloudformation` / `cdkd export` bullets so a YAML-authored template stays YAML on the wire). **18 new unit tests** across [tests/unit/cli/upload-cfn-template.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/upload-cfn-template.test.ts) (constants / upload + PutObject shape / cleanup runs DeleteObject + destroys client / cleanup-failure path / PutObject-failure path / profile + credentials forwarding / us-east-1 URL shape / `findLargeInlineResources` empty / threshold / custom-threshold / missing-Properties guard) and [tests/unit/cli/export-templateurl-upload.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/export-templateurl-upload.test.ts) (size-routing matrix: <=51_200 inline + no-op cleanup / (51_200, 1_048_576] uploads to TemplateURL + actual S3 PutObject / >1_048_576 pre-flight reject names BigLambda + `lambda.Code.fromAsset` hint / cleanup contract: success-path DeleteObject + destroy / failure-path DeleteObject still runs / phase-1 + phase-2 produce the same `cdkd-migrate-tmp/<stack>/<ts>.json` key shape / pre-flight error annotated with caller-supplied phase label "Filtered phase-1 IMPORT" vs "Phase-2 UPDATE"). The existing real-AWS `tests/integration/export/` fixture is unchanged in this PR — the routing logic is fully covered at the unit layer; threading a > 51 KB / > 1 MB fixture through the integ runner is straightforward (50+ tiny `ssm.StringParameter`s) but defers to a follow-up since the unit-test matrix already proves the round-trip end-to-end.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local start-api` mTLS authorizer for API Gateway custom-domain client certs (closes [#446](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/446)). Pre-PR `src/local/http-server.ts` always called `http.createServer`; mTLS was unsupported and `src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts` rejected any non-TOKEN / REQUEST / COGNITO_USER_POOLS Type with a "deferred to a follow-up PR" pointer that bucketed mTLS into the "Authorizer.Type" family (mTLS isn't an Authorizer.Type — it lives at the `AWS::ApiGateway::DomainName.MutualTlsAuthentication` level — so the rejection message was structurally misleading too). Post-PR three new CLI flags `--mtls-truststore <path>` / `--mtls-cert <path>` / `--mtls-key <path>` on `cdkd local start-api`; when ALL THREE are set the server boots `https.createServer({requestCert: true, rejectUnauthorized: true, ca, cert, key, ...})` instead of plain `http.createServer` and the TLS handshake itself enforces the client-cert trust check against the supplied CA bundle (Node's `tls` module rejects unknown-CA / self-signed / missing-cert clients BEFORE the request reaches cdkd's per-request handler — no per-request validation code path in cdkd). Partial flag sets are rejected at CLI parse time via the new `resolveMtlsConfig(options)` helper in [src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts](src/cli/commands/local-start-api.ts) (exported for unit testing) — the server never boots half-configured. The verified peer certificate is surfaced on the Lambda event under `requestContext.identity.clientCert` (REST v1) / `requestContext.authentication.clientCert` (HTTP API v2), matching AWS API Gateway's deployed-mTLS event shape (`{clientCertPem, subjectDN, issuerDN, serialNumber, validity: {notBefore, notAfter}}`). DN formatting follows AWS / OpenSSL convention (CN, OU, O, L, ST, C). Implementation: `src/local/http-server.ts` (new `MtlsServerConfig` interface, https branch in `startApiServer`, `extractClientCert(req)` + `peerCertificateToAws(cert)` + `readMtlsMaterialsFromDisk(opts)` helpers all exported for unit testing; new `scheme: 'http' | 'https'` field on `StartedApiServer` consumed by the listening banner). `src/local/api-gateway-event.ts` (new optional `clientCert?: Record<string, unknown>` on `HttpRequestSnapshot`; REST v1 surfaces it under `requestContext.identity.clientCert`, HTTP API v2 under `requestContext.authentication.clientCert` — the pre-PR `authentication: null` default is preserved when no cert is present). `src/local/authorizer-resolver.ts` rejection message updated to drop mTLS from the deferred-list with a comment naming mTLS as a DomainName-level feature configured via `--mtls-truststore` / `--mtls-cert` / `--mtls-key`. mTLS runs ORTHOGONALLY to the existing TOKEN / REQUEST / COGNITO_USER_POOLS / JWT authorizers — TLS handshake completes first (rejecting unknown-CA clients), then the authorizer pipeline runs against the already-authenticated client. **Scope**: the `--mtls-truststore` file is read once at server boot; the `--watch` hot-reload pipeline does NOT re-read mTLS materials (AWS's `MutualTlsAuthentication.TruststoreVersion` live-update semantics are out of scope — restart the server to pick up a new CA bundle). CLI flag help text + [docs/local-emulation.md](docs/local-emulation.md) carry the openssl recipe (`openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -nodes -keyout ca-key.pem -out ca.pem -subj "/CN=cdkd-local-ca" -days 365` etc.) so users can generate a local CA + server cert + client cert end-to-end and `curl --cacert ca.pem --cert client-cert.pem --key client-key.pem https://localhost:<port>/...` against the server. Tests: 4 new in [tests/unit/local/api-gateway-event.test.ts](tests/unit/local/api-gateway-event.test.ts) (REST v1 + HTTP v2 surface with cert / without cert), 14 new in [tests/unit/local/http-server-mtls.test.ts](tests/unit/local/http-server-mtls.test.ts) (peerCertificateToAws shape extraction across 6 cert shapes + extractClientCert socket-type guard + readMtlsMaterialsFromDisk happy path + ENOENT typed error + scheme=http on plain-HTTP boot + scheme=https on mTLS boot using an openssl-generated fixture cert, with self-skip when openssl is unavailable), 7 new in [tests/unit/cli/local-start-api-mtls.test.ts](tests/unit/cli/local-start-api-mtls.test.ts) (resolveMtlsConfig all-or-none invariant — undefined on no flags, full read on all three, hard-error on any partial set with offending-flag-list in the message, ENOENT typed error). Real-AWS / openssl + curl integ test is intentionally not added in this PR — the openssl handshake is enforced by Node's `tls` module (already battle-tested), not cdkd code, and the unit tests cover every cdkd code path. A follow-up PR may extend `tests/integration/local-start-api/` with a `CDKD_TEST_MTLS=1` variant that pre-generates certs via openssl and asserts curl with `--cert` + `--key` succeeds, curl without fails the TLS handshake.

- ✅ CLI: `cdkd local invoke` / `cdkd local start-api` accept literal Lambda Layer ARNs in `Properties.Layers` (closes [#448](https://github.com/go-to-k/cdkd/issues/448)). Pre-PR `resolveLambdaLayers` in [src/local/lambda-resolver.ts](src/local/lambda-resolver.ts) hard-errored on any `Layers[]` entry that was not a same-stack `Ref` / `Fn::GetAtt` to an `AWS::Lambda::LayerVersion` — every literal-ARN reference (AWS Lambda Powertools, Datadog Extension, shared internal layers, cross-account / cross-region layers) blocked local execution with a "deferred to a follow-up PR" message. Post-PR `Properties.Layers: ['arn:aws:lambda:<region>:<account>:layer:<name>:<version>']` entries are recognized via the new `parseLayerVersionArn` helper (accepts the `aws` / `aws-cn` / `aws-us-gov` partitions; rejects malformed strings with the offending value named) and resolved into a `{kind: 'arn', ...}` variant of the new `ResolvedLambdaLayer` discriminated union (same-stack entries become `{kind: 'asset', ...}`).
